		function hideUpperBn() {
			setWcode('001_001');
			var todayDate = new Date();
			setCookie("UPPER_BN_SHOW", "OK", 1); // 오른쪽 숫자는 쿠키를 유지할 기간(day)을 설정합니다
			$("#upperBnWrap").css("display", "none");
		}

		if (getCookie("UPPER_BN_SHOW") == "") {
			$("#upperBnWrap").css("display","");
		}
		$('#upperBnRoll .upperBnSet').eq( Math.floor(Math.random()*$("#upperBnRoll .upperBnSet").length) ).show();

						var url = location.href;
						var reUrl = url.toLowerCase();
						
						$(document).ready(function () {
							//검색결과
						    if (reUrl.indexOf('/product/search') > -1 && reUrl.indexOf('/product/search/searchkeyword') <= 0) {
								SearchBarRenderingEnable = false;

								if (getParamValue("query") != undefined) {
									$("#query").val($("#hidSearchWord").val());
									fnGetValueDomain($("#hidSearchDomain").val());
									$("#domain").val($("#hidSearchDomain").val());
									$("#qdomain").val($("#hidSearchQdomain").val());
								}
							}
							if (SearchBarRenderingEnable == true) {
								fnSearchBarRendering();
							}
						});

						// 검색어 입력창에 포커스 시
						function SearchBarRenderingEnableSet(enable) {
							//광고 제거
							SearchBarRenderingEnable = enable;
							$("#ulSchScopeOpt").hide(); 
						}

						// 검색어 입력창 광고 노출
						function fnSearchBarRendering() {
							var seardtext = $('#hdSearchBarText').val();
							var bannerLink = $("#hdSearchBarLink").val();

							$('#query').val(seardtext);
							$('#query').addClass("iptTxt iptTxtAd");
							$('#keywordAd').val(bannerLink);
						}

						//검색창 선택 시
						function showLatestSearchList() {
							SearchBarRenderingEnableSet(false);
							if (String($("input#query").val()).length == 0) {
								try{
									srchHistory.show();
								}catch(e){}
								$("#suggestSearchList").hide();
								$("#searchKeyLayer").show();
								$("#latestSearchList").show();
							} else {
								BulletSearchRenewal.InitBulletSearch();
								showSuggestSearchList();
							}
						}

						function hideLatestSearchList() {
							$("#searchKeyLayer").hide();
							$("#latestSearchList").hide();
						}

						//추천검색어
						function showSuggestSearchList() {
							var domainVal = String($("#qdomain").val());
							if (domainVal != '티켓' && domainVal != '블로그' && domainVal != '채널예스' && domainVal != 'STORE' && domainVal != 'UsedGoods') {
								$("#latestSearchList").hide();
								$("#searchKeyLayer").show();
								$("#suggestSearchList").show();
							} else {
								$("#suggestSearchList").hide();
								$("#searchKeyLayer").show();
								$("#latestSearchList").show();
							}
						}

						function hideSuggestSearchList() {
							$("#searchKeyLayer").hide();
							$("#suggestSearchList").hide();
						}
                    </script>
					<span class="schBtn"><button onmouseover="this.className='ovr'" onmouseout="this.className=''" type="submit" title="검색"><span class="yBlind">검색</span></button></span>

					<script type="text/javascript">
						/* 빠른분야 찾기 시작 */
						var quickChkWide = false; //quick menu wide chk
						var submenuId = '';
						var $quickMenu = $("#quickCate");

						$quickMenu.menuAim({
							activate: activeQuickSubmenu,
							deactivate: deactiveQuickSubmenu
						});

						function activeQuickSubmenu(row) {
							var $row = $(row),
							submenuId = $row.attr('data-submenu-id'),
							$submenu = $("#" + submenuId);

							// Show the submenu
							$("#quickCate > li").removeClass("on");
							$(".quickCateSub").css("display", "none");
							$submenu.css("display", "block");
							$row.parent().addClass("on");

							if (!quickChkWide) {
								if ( (document.compatMode==="CSS1Compat") || (navigator.appName != 'Microsoft Internet Explorer') ) {
									$("#quickCateWrap .quickCateLiWrap").css("overflow","hidden");
									$("#quickCateWrap .quickCateLiWrap").stop().animate({width:"664px"},200,"easeInCubic",function(){
										if( $('#quickCateWrap').css("display") == "none" ) {
											$(this).css("width","auto");
										}
										$(this).css({"overflow":"visible","display":""})
									});
								} else {
									$("#quickCateWrap .quickCateLiWrap").css("width","564px");
								}
								quickChkWide = true;
							}
						}

						function deactiveQuickSubmenu(row) {
							var $row = $(row),
							submenuId = $row.attr('data-submenu-id'),
							$submenu = $("#" + submenuId);

							// Hide the submenu and remove the row's highlighted look
							$submenu.css("display", "none");
							$row.parent().removeClass("on");
						}
						/* 빠른분야 찾기 끝 */
                    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var _IS_LOGIN = "False";
    var checkGoodsNo = (typeof (goodsNo) == "undefined") ? "" : goodsNo;
    var checkUrl = "/Product/Goods/" + checkGoodsNo;
    var recentGoods = (recentViewGoods != undefined) ? recentViewGoods.list.sort() : new Array();
    if (location.href.toLowerCase().indexOf(checkUrl.toLowerCase()) == -1) {//상품상세 페이지가 아닌 경우에만 조회 (중복조회 방지)
        GetRecentViewGoodsXhr(true);
    }

    if (_IS_LOGIN == "True") {  //로그인 상태일 경우 마이 예스24 영역 처리
        $("#remoMy").html("마이 예스24");
        $("#remoMyCont").css("display", "block");
    }

    /* 바로24 s */
    $('.yBaro').find('a:first').bind('mouseover focus', function () {
        $(this).next().show();
    });

    $('.yBaro').bind('mouseleave', function () {
        $(this).find('a:first').next().hide();
    });

    $('#remoMy a, .yWingTopBn a').bind('focus', function () {
        $('.yBaro').find('a:first').next().hide();
    });
    
	// ajax cache 막음
	function ajaxNoCache() {
	    $.ajaxSetup({ cache: false, headers: { "cache-control": "no-cache", "pragma": "no-cache" } });
	}

	function RemoveRecentViewGoods(goodsNo) {//최근본상품삭제
	    var index = recentViewGoods.find(goodsNo);
	    if (index != -1) {
	        var params = { "goodsNo": goodsNo, "isLogin": _IS_LOGIN, "useCache": true, "callBackFun": GetRecentViewGoodsXhr };
	        recentViewGoods.delRecentViewGoods(params);
	    }
	}

    function GetRecentViewGoodsXhr(useCache) {//최근본상품조회
        if (recentGoods.length > 0 || (_IS_LOGIN.toLowerCase() == "true" && notCookie == "Y")) {
            $("#remoRctGCont").css("display", "");

            var url = NOW_HTTP_URL + "/Product/Goods/JsonGoodsList";
            var params = { "isLogin": _IS_LOGIN, "useCache": useCache };
            var callbackmethod = RecentViewGoodsDisplay;
            var responseType = "JSON";

            try {
                new XhrUtil(url, params, callbackmethod, responseType);
            } catch (e) {
            }
        }
        else {
            $("#RecentViewGoodsNodata").show();
            $("#ulRecentViewGoods").hide();
            $(".skyPagen").html("");
            $("#RecentViewGoodsCount").html("");
        }
    }

    function RecentViewGoodsDisplay(rtn) {//최근본상품조회결과 화면출력
        var data = null;

        try {
            data = eval("(" + rtn + ")");
        }
        catch (e) {
            data = rtn;
        }

        if (data.recentGoodsCount > 0) {
            var shtml = "";
            var shtmlhide = "";
            var j = 0;
            var idx = 0;

            for (var i = data.recentGoodsCount - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
                if (j % 3 == 0) {
                    shtml += "<ul class='rctGLi' style='display:none'>";
                }
                idx++;

                if (data.recentGoods[i].status != null && data.recentGoods[i].status == "07" && data.recentGoods[i].shopPrice != null && data.recentGoods[i].shopPrice == 1) {
                    data.recentGoods[i].Price = "가격미정";
                }

                if (idx > 2) {
                    shtml += "<li " + shtmlhide + ">\n" +
                        "<a href=\"/Product/Goods/" + data.recentGoods[i].goodsNo + "\" onclick=\"setWcode('003_003_002')\"  class=\"rctLnk\"><img class=\"lazy\" data-original=\"https://image.yes24.com/goods/" + data.recentGoods[i].goodsNo + "/S\" border=\"0\" alt=\"" + data.recentGoods[i].goodsName + "\"/></a>\n" +
                        "<span class=\"rctInfo\">\n" +
                            "<p class=\"rctName\"><a href=\"/Product/Goods/" + data.recentGoods[i].goodsNo + "\" onclick=\"setWcode('003_003_002')\"  >" + data.recentGoods[i].goodsName + "</a></p>\n" +
                            "<p class=\"rctPrice\">" + data.recentGoods[i].Price + "</p>\n" +
                        "</span>\n" +
                    "<a href='javascript:void(0);' onclick='RemoveRecentViewGoods(" + data.recentGoods[i].goodsNo + ")' class=\"btnDel\">최근본상품 삭제</a>\n" +
                    "</li>\n";
                }
                else {
                    shtml += "<li " + shtmlhide + ">\n" +
                       "<a href=\"/Product/Goods/" + data.recentGoods[i].goodsNo + "\" onclick=\"setWcode('003_003_002')\"  class=\"rctLnk\"><img src=\"https://image.yes24.com/goods/" + data.recentGoods[i].goodsNo + "/S\" border=\"0\" alt=\"" + data.recentGoods[i].goodsName + "\"/></a>\n" +
                       "<span class=\"rctInfo\">\n" +
                           "<p class=\"rctName\"><a href=\"/Product/Goods/" + data.recentGoods[i].goodsNo + "\" onclick=\"setWcode('003_003_002')\"  >" + data.recentGoods[i].goodsName + "</a></p>\n" +
                           "<p class=\"rctPrice\">" + data.recentGoods[i].Price + "</p>\n" +
                       "</span>\n" +
                   "<a href='javascript:void(0);' onclick='RemoveRecentViewGoods(" + data.recentGoods[i].goodsNo + ")' class=\"btnDel\">최근본상품 삭제</a>\n" +
                   "</li>\n";
                }
                if (j % 3 == 2 || j == data.recentGoodsCount - 1) {
                    shtml += "</ul>";
                }
                j++;
            }

            $("#ulRecentViewGoods").html(shtml);

            if (data.recentGoodsCount > 9) {
                $("#RecentViewGoodsCount").html("9+");
            } else {
                $("#RecentViewGoodsCount").html(data.recentGoodsCount);
            }

            $('#ulRecentViewGoods').switchDiv({
                current: 0,
                pageBtnsClassSelector: ".gnbSquareBtn",
                pageNumTextSelector: ".yPgNum",
                isShowBtn: true,
                moveEvent: function (obj, settings, index) {
                    setLazyLoad($($("#ulRecentViewGoods ul.rctGLi")[index]).find("img.lazy"), false);
                }
            });

            $("#remoRctGCont li").bind("mouseover focus", function () {
                $(this).attr("class", "on");
            });
            $("#remoRctGCont li").bind("mouseleave", function () {
                $(this).attr("class", "");
            });

            $(".rctPrice").each(function (index) {
                var value =  $(this).text();
                if (value != "가격미정")
                {
                    $(this).text($(this).text().split(/(?=(?:\d{3})+(?:\.|$))/g).join(',') + "원");
                }
            });

            $("#remoThemGCont").hide();
        }
        else {
            $("#RecentViewGoodsNodata").show();
            $("#ulRecentViewGoods").hide();
            $(".skyPagen").html("");
            $("#RecentViewGoodsCount").html("");
        }
    }
</script>

		<script type="text/javascript">
			function closePartnerBn(close) {
				$("#bnPartnerWing").css({ "display": "none" });
				setCookie("Yes24_PartnerWingRightArea", "OK", 1);
			}
			function setCookiePartnerWingBn() {
				var name = "PartnerWingArea";
				var value = "OK";
				var expiredays = 1;
				var todayDate = new Date();
				todayDate.setDate(todayDate.getDate() + expiredays);
				document.cookie = name + "=" + escape(value) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + "; domain=.yes24.com;"
				closePartnerBn();
			}
			function OAS_RICHTest() {
				try{
					if (OAS_RICH.toString().indexOf("//adgirl.yes24.com/RealMedia/ads/Creatives/default/empty.gif") <= 0) {
						if (getCookie("Yes24_PartnerWingRightArea") != "OK") {
							OAS_RICH("Right");
							$("#bnPartnerWing a").eq(1).addClass("lnk_bn");
						}
						else{
							$("#bnPartnerWing").css({ "display": "none" });
						}
					} else {
						$("#bnPartnerWing").css({ "display": "none" });
					}
				} catch (e) { }
			}

	<script>
		var IsMania = 'False';
	    var IsHyndaiCardIssue = 'False';
		var IsPlatinum = 'False';
		var regQPop = false;
		var regBpop = false;
		var showHCPop = false;
		if (IsPlatinum == 'True' && IsHyndaiCardIssue != 'True' && getCookie("yes24_Mania_hyundaiCardPlcc_pop") == "") {
			showHCPop = true;
		}
		if ($("#divYes24PartnerEvent_Mania").length > 0) {
			regQPop = true;
		}
		if ($("#divYes24BookClubEvent_Mania").length > 0) {
			regBpop = true;
        }

        if (getCookie("yes24_Mania_gift_pop") == "" && regQPop) {
			//마니아 퀴즈팝업 등록 & 오늘은 그만보기 클릭 X
			$("#maniaQuizPop").attr('style', '');
			$("#hyundaiPlccPopUpBanner").attr('style', 'display:none;');
			$("#bookclubFirstOrdPopUpBanner").attr('style', 'display:none;');
		}
        else if (getCookie("yes24_Mania_gift_pop") != "" && regQPop) {
			//마니아 퀴즈팝업 등록 & 오늘은 그만보기 클릭 O
            if (showHCPop) {
				$("#hyundaiPlccPopUpBanner").attr('style', '');
				$("#bookclubManiaPop").attr('style', 'display:none;');
			}
			else if (IsPlatinum != 'True' && IsMania == 'True') {
				$("#bookclubManiaPop").attr('style', '');
			}
			else {
				$("#bookclubFirstOrdPopUpBanner").attr('style', '');
			}
		}
        else if (!regQPop && getCookie("yes24_Mania_bookclub_pop") == "" && regBpop) {
			//마니아퀴즈 팝업 등록 X & 크레마클럽 마니아 등록
			$("#bookclubManiaPop").attr('style', '');
			$("#hyundaiPlccPopUpBanner").attr('style', 'display:none;');
			$("#bookclubFirstOrdPopUpBanner").attr('style', 'display:none;');
		}
        else if (!regQPop && (!regBpop || getCookie("yes24_Mania_bookclub_pop") != "")) {
            if (showHCPop) {
                $("#hyundaiPlccPopUpBanner").attr('style', '');
                $("#bookclubManiaPop").attr('style', 'display:none;');
            }
            else {
                $("#bookclubFirstOrdPopUpBanner").attr('style', '');
            }
        }

        if (getCookie("yes24_Mania_bookclub_pop") == "" && $("#divYes24BookClubEvent_Mania").css("display") == "none" && regBpop){
			$('#divYes24BookClubEvent_Mania').show();
		}

		function closeWindow__Mania_BookClub_pop() {
			var todayDate = new Date();
			setCookieOneDay("yes24_Mania_bookclub_pop", "OK", 24 - todayDate.getHours()); // 오른쪽 숫자는 쿠키를 유지할 기간(day)을 설정합니다
			$("#divYes24BookClubEvent_Mania").hide();
        }
        function closeWindow__Mania_HyundaiCardPlcc_pop() {
            var todayDate = new Date();
            setCookieOneDay("yes24_Mania_hyundaiCardPlcc_pop", "OK", 24 - todayDate.getHours()); 
            $("#divYes24HyundaiCardPlcc_Mania").hide();
        }
        function closeWindow__bookclubFirstOrdPop() {
			var todayDate = new Date();
            todayDate.setDate(todayDate.getDate() + 7);
            document.cookie = "yes24_bookclubFirstOrd_pop=" + escape("OK") + "; path=/;domain=.yes24.com;expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";";
            $("#divYes24bookclubFirstOrdPop").hide();
        }
    </script>

<script language ="javascript" type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() {
        expend_menu("001");
    });
    emptyAdBanner();
    function emptyAdBanner() {
        var adImg1 = $("#bestseller_ad1 a img").attr("src");
        var adImg2 = $("#bestseller_ad2 a img").attr("src");
        var adEmptyImg = "//adgirl.yes24.com/RealMedia/ads/Creatives/default/empty.gif";
        if (adImg1.includes(adEmptyImg)) {
            $("#bestseller_ad1").attr("class", "");
        }
        if (adImg2.includes(adEmptyImg)) {
            $("#bestseller_ad2").attr("class", "");
        }
    }
    
    function open_subDepth(disno, e) {
        add_subDepth(disno);
                
        
        if (e.stopPropagation) {
            e.stopPropagation(); 
        } 
        e.cancelBubble = true;
    }
    
    function add_subDepth(dispno, full_dispno) {
        var obj = $('#category' + dispno);
        var list = $(obj).find("ul:first");
        if ($(list).length > 0) {
            $(list).toggle();
            if (full_dispno != null) {
                if (dispno.length < full_dispno.length) {
                    sub_dispno = full_dispno.substring(0,dispno.length + 3);
                    add_subDepth(sub_dispno, full_dispno);
                }
            }     
        } else {
            
            		
            if (dispno != '') {
                $.get("category/BestSellerSubCategory/" + dispno + "?SumGb=" + "06", function(data) {
                    $(obj).append(data);
                    if (full_dispno != null) {
	                    if (dispno.length < full_dispno.length) {
	                        sub_dispno = full_dispno.substring(0,dispno.length + 3);
		                    add_subDepth(sub_dispno, full_dispno);
		                }
		            }
                });
            }
            
        }
        $(obj).toggleClass("open");
    }
    
    function expend_menu(dispno) {
        if(dispno.length > 2)
		    add_subDepth(dispno.substring(0,3), dispno);
    }
</script>

<script> 
    bestday_change();
    function bestday_change() {
        var lastday = lastday_of_month($("#bestyear").val(), $("#bestmonth").val());
        var bestday = document.getElementById("bestday");
        if(bestday != null){
            for (var i = 28; i <= 31; i++) {
                if (lastday < i) {
                    $("#optday" + i).hide();
                }
                else {
                    $("#optday" + i).show();
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    function goto_bestseller(type) {
        var year = $("#bestyear").val();
        var month = $("#bestmonth").val();
        if (type == "07") {
            var day = $("#bestday").val();
            location.href = "/24/category/bestseller?CategoryNumber=001&sumgb=07&year=" + year + "&month=" + month + "&day=" + day;
        }
        else if (type == "08") {
            var week = $("#bestweek").val();
            location.href = "/24/category/bestseller?CategoryNumber=001&sumgb=08&year=" + year + "&month=" + month + "&week=" + week + "&day=1";
        }
        else if (type == "09") {
        location.href = "/24/category/bestseller?CategoryNumber=001&sumgb=09&year=" + year + "&month=" + month;
        }
    }


    function excludOptUrl() {
        var eo = "INCLUDE";
        if (eo == "INCLUDE") {
            location.href = "/24/category/bestseller?CategoryNumber=002&EO=1";
        }
        else {
            location.href = "/24/category/bestseller?CategoryNumber=002&EO=0";
        }
    }

</script>

        $(diskNoList).each(function () {

                var oInput = document.createElement("INPUT");

                oInput.id = "chkTrackList";
                oInput.name = "chkTrackList";

                form.appendChild(oInput);
            }
        });

        oInput = document.createElement("INPUT");
        oInput.type = "hidden";
        oInput.id = "goodsNo";
        oInput.name = "goodsNo";
        oInput.value = goodsNo;
        form.appendChild(oInput);

        oInput.type = "hidden";

        form.target = 'PreMusicPlay';

        form.submit();
    }
    function openEBookPreview(ebookcode, goodsno) {
        var width = 790;
        var height = 880;
        var c = 0;
        var d = 0;

        if (screen.width >= screen.height) {
            if (screen.width <= 1024 || screen.height <= 768) {
                c = 50;
                d = 30;
                width = 618;
                height = 708;
            } else {
                c = 100;
                d = 30;
            }
        } else {
            c = 30;
            d = 30;
        }

        var returnurl = NOW_HTTP_URL + "/24/goods/" + goodsno;
        var url = "http://epreview.yes24.com/preview/viewer/viewer.html?ebookcode=" + ebookcode + "&dm=yes24.com" + "&returnURL=" + encodeURIComponent(returnurl);

        window.open(url, "yes24preview", "menubar=no,status=no,toolbar=no,scrolling=no,resizable=yes,width=" + width + ",height=" + height + ", top=" + c + ",left=" + d);
    }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    //레이어를 오픈한다.
    function Open_DetailViewLayer(locationIndex, goodsNo) {

        yes24GU.checkValidGoods(goodsNo, false,
            function (isSuccess, data) {
                if (isSuccess) {
                    Show_DetailViewLayer(locationIndex, goodsNo);
                }
                else {
                    yes24GU.showCartError(data.ErrorCodes[0], data.Goods[0], '');
                }
            },
            function (data) { }
        );
    }

    function Show_DetailViewLayer(locationIndex, goodsNo) {
        if (locationIndex % 2 == 1)
            locationIndex = locationIndex - 1;

        var layerLocation = $("#location_" + locationIndex);

        if (layerLocation == null)
            return;

        var layer = document.createElement("div");
        document.body.appendChild(layer);

        if ($(layer) != null)
            $(layer).css("position", "relative");

        var viewDetailLayer = $("#viewDetailLayer");

        if (viewDetailLayer == null)
            return;

        var x = layerLocation.offset().left + 20;
        var y = layerLocation.offset().top - 5;

        viewDetailLayer.css("left", x);
        viewDetailLayer.css("top", y);

        $.get("/24/Content/Popup/ViewDetailLayer.aspx?GoodsNo=" + goodsNo + "&CategoryNumber=001", function (data) {
            viewDetailLayer.ready(function () {
                viewDetailLayer.html(data);
            });
        });

        viewDetailLayer.show();
    }

    function Close_DetailViewLayer() {
        var viewDetailLayer = $("#viewDetailLayer");
        if (viewDetailLayer == null)
            return;

        viewDetailLayer.hide();
    }

    $(document).ready(function () {
        // Dfinery 디파이너리 카테고리 페이지뷰 로그.
        try {
            var dfineryLogProduct = new dfinery.product('-', '-', 1, 1, 1, '001');
            dfinery.setdfineryLog("abx_category_view", dfineryLogProduct, {"category": '001'});
            /*
            if (typeof (is_debug) !== 'undefined' && is_debug) {
                console.log('dfinery: abx_category_view');
            }
            */
        } catch (e) {

        }
    });
</script>

    function dcPopup(url, name, w, h) {
        var x = (screen.availWidth / 2) - (w / 2);
        var y = (screen.availHeight / 2) - (h / 2);
        return window.open(url, name, "toolbar=no,resizable=yes,scrollbars=yes,status=no,location=no,left=" + x + ",top=" + y + ",width=" + w + ",height=" + h);
    }

<script type="text/javascript">
    var cosem_Request = function () {
        var cookieDay = 7; // 쿠키설정 날짜
        var accountCode = "825";
        this.getParameter = function (name) {
            var rtnval = ''; var nowAddress = unescape(location.href); var parameters = (nowAddress.slice(nowAddress.indexOf('?') + 1, nowAddress.length)).split('&');
            for (var i = 0; i < parameters.length; i++) { var varName = parameters[i].split('=')[0]; if (varName.toUpperCase() == name.toUpperCase()) { rtnval = parameters[i].split('=')[1]; break; }; }; return rtnval;
        }
        this.imageURL = function () {
            var cosem = this.getParameter('cosemkid'); var cosem_kid = ""; var cosemProtocol = (location.protocol == "https:") ? "https:" : "http:";
            if (cosem.length == 0) cosem = this.getParameter('cosem');
            if (cosem.length > 0) {
                cosem_kid = "&kid=" + cosem + "&referer=" + encodeURIComponent(location.href);
                var image = new Image(); image.src = cosemProtocol + "//" + "tracking.icomas.co.kr" + "/Script/script3.php" + "?aid=" + accountCode + "&ctime=" + cookieDay + cosem_kid;
            };
        };
        this.tracking = function () { var obj = this; setTimeout(function () { obj.imageURL(); }, 10); };
    };
    var cosemRequest = new cosem_Request();
    cosemRequest.tracking();


    function cosemConvert(rn, amt, pc, pa, pp, pg, etc) {
        var cosemProtocol = (location.protocol == "https:") ? "https:" : "http:";
        var image = new Image();
        var accountCode = "825";
        var imageURL = cosemProtocol + "//" + "tracking.icomas.co.kr";
        imageURL += "/Script/action3.php" + "?aid=" + accountCode + "&rn=" + encodeURI(rn);
        imageURL += "&amt=" + amt + "&pc=" + encodeURI(pc) + "&pa=" + pa + "&pp=" + pp + "&pg=" + encodeURI(pg) + "&etc=" + encodeURI(etc);
        image.src = imageURL;
    }

    var sUrl = location.href.toLowerCase();
    if (sUrl.indexOf('registerend.aspx') > -1) {
        setTimeout(function () {
            cosemConvert("", 0, "회원가입", 0, 0, location.href, "");
        }, 10);
    }
</script>
